msg:We booked 4 rooms for this trip, 2 king-size rooms and 2 standard rooms. The price of the standard room is higher than that of the king-size room, which I didn't expect. Usually they are the same price, and the price is different on weekdays and Fridays and Saturdays, which I can understand. After checking in, I found that the king-size room is quite small, and the standard room is slightly larger. No wonder the prices of the 2 standard rooms are different. The most expensive one is a slightly larger standard room. It was booked online, so the price is fixed. The other room is a king-size room and I asked to change it to a standard room. I paid the difference of 260 when I checked in. The prices on the first and second days are different. It is cheaper than the standard room booked online, so it is also smaller. Although small, it has everything. There is a sterilizer in each room, which is very friendly for families like us with children. Every time I go out, I bring a machine, and I sterilize them one by one. This time, I can sterilize all the bottles at once like at home, so we are very satisfied with this. There is also a coffee machine that should be the model of Nestle's dolce gusto fully automatic home smart capsule. However, after we made a cup on the last day, we found that the machine was leaking or something. A lot of coffee juice leaked out... I hope it can be fixed. There is also a Xiaomi air purifier in each room, which is pretty good. The front desk explained to me when I checked in that the room was upgraded to a higher level. They are all view rooms... but they are relatively small. There are free fruits replenished every day. The drinks in the refrigerator are free to drink and replenished every day. Any used ones in the room will be replenished the next day. Water can be taken at will in the corridor on each floor. There is hot mineral water in the lobby on the first floor. It is really good news for parents. You can take a bottle of medicine at any time! ! ! There is a small place for children to play in the lobby on the first floor. It seems a bit small... I hope it can be made bigger. I would like to thank Ding Xin at the front desk for contacting me when placing the order and communicating with me. I may choose this store next time. It is suggested that the breakfast can be richer. There may be limited space, but it is great to have different hot drinks for breakfast. The service of the staff is very good and enthusiastic
